(function() {
  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch && sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj && typeof obj === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function(k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  }

  function getAppName() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.applicationName", window);
  }

  function getMidasConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }

  function getMidasCfgVal(cfgName) {
    var cfg = getMidasConfig();
    var appName = getAppName();
    var pageCfgKey = appName + "-" + cfgName;
    return cfg[pageCfgKey] || cfg[cfgName];
  }

  function loadScript(scriptUrl) {
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

  function loadAds() {
    if (!loadAds.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-midas-display");
      loadAds.loaded = true;
      var displayAds = getMidasCfgVal("displayAds") !== "false";
      if (displayAds) {
        var MDABT = getCookie("MDABT");
        var midasDisplayScript =
          getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABT) ||
          getMidasCfgVal("midasDisplayScript");
        var gptUrl = "//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js";
        if (getMidasCfgVal("loadDisplayScript") !== "false") {
          loadScript(midasDisplayScript);
        }
        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  }

  function loadS2SScripts() {
    if (!loadS2SScripts.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-s2s-midas-scripts");
      loadS2SScripts.loaded = true;
      var MDABTS2S = getCookie("MDABTS2S");
      var midasS2SScript =
        getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABTS2S) || getMidasCfgVal("midasS2SScript");
      loadScript(midasS2SScript);
    }
  }

  function addPerfMark(markName){
    var hasPerfMark = !!get("performance.mark", window);
    if (hasPerfMark) {
      // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
      window.performance.mark(markName);
    }
  }
  var loadS2SEvent =
    getCookie("loadS2SEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadS2SEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadS2SEvent") ||
    "hasS2SPayload";

  var loadEvent =
    getCookie("loadEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadEvent") ||
    "instant";
  window._wml.adLoader = (function() {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        addPerfMark('fire-event-' + eventName);
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function(listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      },
    };
  })();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent("instant"); // Default load ads immediately
})();

is a great 32” TV, one of the best on the market.  I currently own 2 of these and had never had a Roku TV before these.  This was a game changer.  I had used Firesticks and Chromecast before, but love the functionality of Roku.  

It integrates your live TV and free Pluto TV channels.  My favorite feature is the Roku app that you can download and use as a remote!  No longer searching for those darn things.  The TV is high quality and light weight.  For the size, the sound is good quality as well.  I viewed this tv in store next to other 32” TVs and it was nearly impossible to tell the difference.  When my larger TVs need replaced, I&#39;ll be looking to Onn and Roku!  

Highlights
-Roku
-Lightweight 
-Most affordable option
-Can be wall mounted or use included legs
-Quality Sound</p></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;transition:0s;width:100000px;height:100000px"></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;transition:0s;width:200%;height:200%"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="revealer-footer text-center border"><button class="button caret-arrow button--link" data-automation-id="button" data-tl-id="" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="Collapsable-1616987895075" aria-label="See more" type="button"><span class="button-wrapper">See more</span></button></div></div></div><div class="review-body-media-modal"><div><button class="button button--link" data-automation-id="button" data-tl-id="button" aria-current="false" type="button"><span class="button-wrapper"><img width="80" height="80" class="review-media-thumbnail" src="//i5.walmartimages.com/dfw/6e29e393-7b9d/k2-_8ce4f4b1-1d90-4006-b87a-17ffcdb960ca.v1.bin?odnWidth=100&amp;odnHeight=100&amp;odnBg=000" alt="User uploaded thumbnail, 1 of 1"/></span></button></div></div></div><div class="review-footer"><div class="badges"><div class="review-user"><span class="visuallyhidden">Reviewed by EKKJ</span><span itemprop="author" class="review-footer-userNickname">EKKJ</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ReviewHelpfulness "><div class="helpful-voting"><span class="helpful-text">Helpful?</span><button class="button review-help-link s-margin-top yes-vote button--link" data-automation-id="button" data-tl-id="ReviewHelpfulness-YesCount" aria-label="Like review by EKKJ,

itemprop="name" class="review-title font-bold">Love this smart TV!</h3></div><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/Rating"><meta itemprop="worstRating" content="1"/><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></div><div class="review-date"><span itemprop="datePublished" content="February 20, 2020" class="review-date-submissionTime">February 20, 2020</span></div><div class="review-body"><div itemprop="reviewBody" class="review-description"><div><div class="collapsable content-fadeout review-body-text has-toggle" style="min-height:125px" id="Collapsable-1616987895079"><div class="collapsable-content-container"><div><div class="review-text"><p>This TV is amazing! It works perfectly in my bedroom on my dresser! I love that I don&#39;t have to connect a device to this and everything is prebuilt into the TV. The setup was quick and easy. The TV automatically found my internet and I just needed to put my password in, it was so easy to connect. I do have a slow internet connection, but it doesn&#39;t seem to affect this Roku TV. It needed to update right after setup, but that took less than five minutes. After the update, there was a short video that automatically played a clip showing how to use the TV and remote. Channels can be added very quickly. There is a lot of free games and channels to watch television, so even if you don&#39;t have a paid streaming service it is still worth it. You can hook up an antenna, gaming console or cable up as well, but I haven&#39;t used it for any of those yet. The picture and sound quality are really good. I can have the volume at a low setting and still hear it good. I very rarely need the volume higher than 12. When turning it off, it was a slow shutdown and counts down from three then turns off. I like that because I feel like it&#39;s better on the TV instead of an instant shutdown. It has three HDMI ports, one USB port, one RF port, one optical port and a headphone jack on the side of the TV. There is a button on the bottom of the TV that you can press to turn the TV on or switch inputs, but you will need the remote for anything else. The remote is easy to use. The volume is on the right side of the remote. It comes with four assigned shortcut buttons. I find these buttons annoying since I don&#39;t have two out of the four channels. It is very easy to accidentally press those buttons and interrupt whatever you were doing. I wish I could at the very least reassign those buttons to channels that I use. I installed the Roku app on my phone and use it as a remote also. It comes with plastic legs to mount on the bottom of the TV, that just screw on the bottom. It can also be mounted to the wall as well.</p></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div television</h3></div><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/Rating"><meta itemprop="worstRating" content="1"/><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta class="review-body"><div itemprop="reviewBody" class="review-description"><div><div class="collapsable content-fadeout review-body-text has-toggle" style="min-height:125px" id="Collapsable-1616987895080"><div class="collapsable-content-container"><div><div class="review-text"><p>The ONN ROKU TV 32” Smart TV Came well packaged with plenty of padding to protect the tv during shipping. The TV comes with legs that can be attached very easily if you were going to place it on a tv stand. The tv can also be mounted on the wall using a standard wall mount kit. The tv uses a standard 200x100mm bolt pattern on the back. The tv has hook ups for the following, 1 cable line in, 1 USB port, 3 HDMI ports, 1 optical port and RCA connections as well.</p><p>The tv has a very clear picture and has easy on-screen quick start instructions. It also comes with a quick start guide. The tv can be connected to an internet connection for use with different tv apps. The tv is compatible with many online movie providers and websites for streaming. The ONN Smart TV has 720p resolution and stereo sound with 2 built in speakers. The tv comes with a simple to use remote with easy to identify and use buttons, it does come with batteries as well. This tv shows a great picture, we have HD on our other tv and the picture comes in great. The pixels are nice for a clear picture. We have this 32&#34; Class HD in our grandchildren&#39;s room for after school tv time or online gaming. I do recommend this Onn 720p LED tv for any room of your home or office. We may look into getting another one at this price and quality for our kitchen. Very nice sound quality. Please see photos attached and the nice little remote control that comes with this set. </p><p>Overall, the tv is well made and the multiple apps that can be used both free and paid make this a great mid-size television.</p></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div contents exposed</h3></div><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/Rating"><meta itemprop="worstRating" content="1"/><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta class="verified">Verified purchase</div></div><div class="review-body"><div itemprop="reviewBody" class="review-description"><div><div class="collapsable content-fadeout review-body-text has-toggle" style="min-height:125px" id="Collapsable-1616987895082"><div class="collapsable-content-container"><div><div class="review-text"><p>The TV works still so that&#39;s why I&#39;m giving it 43stars, but this item is shipped in it&#39;s actual physical packaging, no extra box over it to protect it. As such, when mine was delivered on a rainy Saturday while we were running errands, for some reason it was left lying flat on the wet ground, not under the overhang right by that door. Not inside the screen door that it likely would have fit pretty decently inside and would have don&#39;t a decent job of covering it. Needless to say, the outer box of a TV that is being given as a gift can no longer be wrapped in paper and given, now I have to just put a big gift bag over the TV and be really careful not to damage it while transporting it to holiday festivities. I actually recall selecting the box that says &#34;this is a gift&#34;. I never would have expected it to show up in it&#39;s actual box after selecting that option. 

As you can see from the pictures, the box couldn&#39;t be saved.

To say I&#39;m disappointed is an understatement.
Great job on the fast shipping though.</p></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div
